2b2(ka): ston pa gnhen rab mi bo na/ sa bdag dbang chen gyi so brang na/ 'dul byed sprul pa'i gnas mchog/ rin po cha grangs ma spungs pa'i gnas mchog/ lo panga dbu lnga'i gzhal /

2b4(ka): grangs med 'byung ba rim gyis brtsegs pa'i dkyil 'khor che/ thags ri nag po gcig gis yongs su bskor ba'i steng / bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gdung bdun lnga gsum gnas pa/

3a1(ka): dara mtshen b d sprin ltar gtibg/ nag po ra bara byed rgyan pas la/ sngon po gsu 'di mkhar badal tcog du b la/ ser po ren chen skyed mo tshal chen ni/ mtshcung / 
3a2(ka): rin chen grangs mang brtol pa la/ lha klungs gtod chen mo che bzhi gnas/ de'i nang du skyed mo'i tshal chen ni/ snang srid go 'byed rig bzhi'i 'od du gsal/ de'i nang ni khyams khang 
3a3(ka): khra bo la/ gzhi ma mthing nag rgya mtsho bon gyi dbyings/ phyogs bzhi'i kha gnon mchod rten chen po bzhi/ rin chen gtsal bkram gling chung gram pa la/ sa dbang dpal gyi 
3a4(ka): gter chen sna tshogs rdol/ de'i nang na g.sung drung gdan chen ni/ mkha' la lha gnas sum hu rtsa drug gi/ gdan chen g.sung drung sum cu rtsa drug la/ gling gi tshul du so brang 
3a5(ka): yod d// shar phyogs lus 'phags mi dga' mongs na yang / kun 'dul byin gyis brlabs kyi brag chen zla 'ag na/ byams pa chen po'i ting 'dzin rnyed par 'gyur ro// byang gi sgra / 
3a6(ka): mi snyan na zhe sdang che na yang / kun grol rtags su shing chen a khod na/ snying rje chen po'i ngang la gnas par 'gyur ro// nub kyi ban glang mi dga' rgongs na yang / kun rig 
3b1(ka): byein gyis brlabs kyi m chen dmu nags na/ dga' ba chen po'i nga la gnas par 'gyur ro// lho'i 'dzam bling brel 'phong kcheng na yang / kun 'dzom khyen gyis brlabs kyi / 
3b2(ka): gngs chen ti ca na/ btang snyoms chen po'i nga la gnas par 'gyur ro// kun 'dul rtags su brag la rin chen rkang bzhi gyis/ kun sgrol rtags su shing la byung gi lam bzhi / 
3b3(ka): d/ kun rigs rtags su me las drod kyi dpal bzhi 'bar/ kun 'djoms rtags su gngs la khrus kyi chab bzhi byab/ phyogs bzhi'i 'byung ba kha gnon rigs bthun ni/ zung 
3b4(ka): bzhi so brang mkha' la 'phags tsam na/ ngo mtshar lha'i re bzhi lta bur 'gyur/ bar khyams gzhal yas de ltar gnas pa'i/ phyogs bzhi'i 'byung ba kha gnon rigs bzhi' 
3b5(ka): mchod rten rang par rgyas pa ni/ re rab kha gnon mchod nyen chen po bzhi/ shar na g.sung drung brtsegs pa'o// byang na 'khor lo bsgyur ba'o// thub na bde ldan prna'o// lho na ran

4a1(ka): / y/ chen po na/ ston pa gnhen rab mo bo bzhugs pa'i/ 'khor gyi dam pa g.yung dung sems dpa' lnga stong lnga brgya dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// yi sangs rgyas pa'i /

4b1(ka): dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// s+dzu 'phrul me lha bzhi dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// me skyong brgyad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// me len chen mo brgyad dang thabs / 
4b2(ka): gcig tu bzhugs so// shing thun ma bzhi dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// rlung lha bzhi dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// sgo ma chen mo bzhi dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so//

4b6(ka): thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// zhing khams kyi rgyal ba rnam brgyad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// gnam gyi lha gsas brgyad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// re rab kyi / 
5a1(ka): dpal dung brgyad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs'o// rgya mtsho' klung skyed brgyad dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs'o// gnam gyi lha men brgyad dang thabs gcig tu /

5a3(ka): shing khams kyi rgyal po lnga dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// byang chu khams kyi rgyal po lnga dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// nub lcags khams kyi rgyal po lnga dang thabs

5a5(ka): drug cu dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs'so// gnam gyi lha bon bcso lnga dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs'so// sa ya klu bon bco lngadang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// bar gyi m bon 
5a6(ka): bco lnga dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// sa bdag dbang chen nyi shu dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// g.sung drung kha sum hu rtsa drug gi lha tshogs bar ma brgya brgya chu dang thabs / 
5b1(ka): gcig tu bzhugs so// kun 'dul bka' nyan 'byung skyong sum cungs bzhi dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// kun sgrol bka' nyan regs pa drug cu dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs /

6a1(ka): con po dag pa khrus kyi bum pa can dang / de las sogs pa'i 'khor gyi dam pa thams cad kyis/ gzugs mdzes pa'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi shun sul/ sgra snyan / 
6a2(ka): pa'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi shu ni bsgrags/ drai zhim pa'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi shu ni blhams/ ri brda' ba'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi hu ni bshams/ rig 'jams pa'i mchod 
6a3(ka): pa bdun brgya nyi shu na sas/ ngag dag pa'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi shu ni brjod/ yid dag pa'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi bhu ni dmigs/ lus dag pa'i mchod pa bdun brgya nyi shu ni 
6a4(ka): btud nas zhus sam gsol pa/ mkhyen pa'i ye shes g.yung drung brtan pa'i srog/ sku mtshan dpe byad bzang po sum su'i dpal 'bar che/ dpe byad bzang po brgyad kus rab brgyan /

6b6(ka): sa bdag yi brten khyab byed de las/ sprul pa'i pho nya dang 'khor ba bsam la 'das pas 'jig rten bskyed cing brkyang na/ sa gzhi rin po che'i dpal dang / sems can spyi mthun gyi / 
7a1(ka): bzgon dang / 'byung ba lnga'i mna' bdag dang / gtsug lag rig pa'i gnas chen mdzad do// de nas sems can las dang bye brag lus kyis/ lha ye lung ni bsdus/ srid / 
7a2(ka): pa'i rgyud ni bshigs/ ston pa'i bstan pa ni gshegs/ sa bdag gi mnga' dbang zhi 'das so// de nas bar gyi bskal pa nyi shus mtho bcad dang zur bskal tsam zhig gnas/ dus 'di/

7a5(ka): khri'i gnas lnga'i sred pa sras po dgu mo dgu las sogs dpag tu med par sprul lo// gnhen rab kyis sprul pa pyung nas 'dul ba'i gnhen bye ba 'bum phrag grangs med par mdzad do//

7b3(ka): yul dang lnga'o// de la gung drug lha rtsi srid pa'i yul de ni/ da lha'i gnas rigs lnga'i grung du gyur pa la/ lnga po de dag con can du bzhag nas/ bon nyid bdal ba'i grung du gyur pa dang 
7b4(ka): drug go/ bon can du bnhag pa gang zhe na/ de lngar gnas pa'i lha dang gnas de dag/ thugs rje dang smon lam gyi mtha' brtan nas/ srid pa'i rgyal po ma mdzad pa dang mdzad pa dang // 
7b5(ka): bstan pa dang ston pa rje rab ston pa'i phyir ro// ban bdal po'i grung do ni/ lnga po de'i ngo bo nyid las/ srid pa'i rgyal po ye zhes kyi bdag nyid/ dus mtha' med par 'khor ba ma stong bar / 
7b6(ka): du bzhugs nas/ sku dang ye shes 'gyur ba med pa'o// lha rtsi ni 'khor ba'i lha dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i lha'i/ gnas rigs thams cad kyi rtsi mor gyur pa'o// srid pa'i yul ni// 
8a1(ka): yu/ sgyu ma 'khor ba'i sred pa ma yin gyis/ sred pa thams cad kyi rgyal po sangs po 'brum khri'i yul lo// de'i phyir na gung drug lha tser srid pa'i yul ning khams chen po / 
8a2(ka): de ni/ rgya khyen nam mkha' tshad dang mtshungs pa yin te/ srid pa mkha' lding gi phyogs gcig pa/ sngon bu g.su rtsi shal gyi gsas mkhar de la/ dper na 'u gu'i ma bcad kyi /

8a5(ka): khams dam pa ni/ rlabs chen bya khyung rgyal po'i gdan khri la/ srid pa'i rgyal po 'bum khri bzhugs/ de las spul pa'i sku mchog bzhi bskyed/ bar lha 'od gsal g.sung drungs

8b1(ka): bzhugs nas/ bar lha 'di gsal g.yung dung sems dpa' la/ kun s+dzob bden par sgra yi rig pa ston/ don dam bden par yi mkhyen theg pa'i/ mi 'jig stobs bcu bskyed par /

8b3(ka): bya/ ye dbal mthu stobs rgyal po sku bzhugs nas/ 'og men gnam gyi ba thu stobs can rnams la/ kun s+dzob bden par nang gi rig pa ston/ don dam bden par ye dbang theg 
8b4(ka): pa'i/ ting 'dzin yan lag drug cu bskyed/ mgon btsun phya'i grong khyer chen po nas/ thugs rjes kun skyobs sman gyi gss mkhar du / nam mkha'i ba mo che'i gdan khri la/

9a1(ka): gser gyi rna thal bsgol pa'i khri steng nas/ srid pa brten pa'i sa 'dzin zhes kyang bya/ ye dbangsa'i rgyal po sku bzhugs pas/ srid pa'i 'khor sde bsam du med pa la// /

9a3(ka): gyi gsas mkhar nas/ srid pa rlabs gcod spyi rje'i khri steng du/ srid pa'i rgyal po sangs po sku bzhugs pas/ dag pa'i srid pa'i rgyal po mu med la/ kun s+dzob bden par 'khor lo /

9b1(ka): gser gyi me tog pul nas zhus pa'i mdo/ rje cig srid pa'i rgyal po sangs po 'bum khri lags/ khams gsum las kyi 'khor ba'i sems can rnams/ nges pa'i don dam ma

9b4(ka): dung yi dbang zhus pazhin tu legs/ dus 'dir bdag gi srid pa'i rgyal po mdzad pa la/ khams gsum las kyi 'khor ba'i sems can nyon mongs 'di/ nges don bstan kyang mi go 
9b5(ka): shin tu rmongs/ bdud kyi chu bzhs thar med sbyong pa la/ khyod kyi phan gyis gdag lugs bstan pa ni/ sku'i srid pa'i rgyal po chen po gcig/ nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dus la bab pa 
9b6(ka): yin/ thugs rjes sprul pa'i srid pa po dgu mo dgu dang / so dbon mo dpon sum brgya rtsa brgyad dang / dbang chen 'khor lo bsgyur ba brgya dang bcu dang / prin las mtha' yas 
10a1(ka): bsgrub pa gnyis brgya nyi bhu dang / thugs rje'i sding 'debs bdun brgya bzhi bcu dang / de las gyis pa srid pa'i rgyal po ni/ bsam du med pa'i tshogs su sku sprul la// /

10a3(ka): la phob/ nyon mongs sems can las kyis rgas la dga'/ rgas la phan gdag khab sgo' dpal kha sphyis/ sdug bsngal sems can lus blang na la dga'/ na la phan gdag lo

10b1(ka): khams skur ston la/ kun 'bum go phyis sems can 'gro don mdzad/ 'dul ba'i dus la bab pas bstan par ran/ smon lam nus mthu sad pas 'grub par 'gyur/ thugs 
10b2(ka): rjes sems bskyed yod pas mdzad par rig/ de skad sangs po 'byum khris bka' stsal nas/ rje'i gsungs pa ci bzhin mdzad pa'i phyir/ srid pa yi sangs zhing khams chen por byen/

11b3(kha): bzhugs/ mdzad pa'i gnhen rab drug cu dang / khams lnga'i rdje blon nyi shu sogs/ de ltar phyi skor lha tshogs gnas/ phyi yi skyed mo tshal chen la/ lo zla zhag dang za ma yi/ sa 
11b4(kha): bdag dpal mgon mchod pa 'brul/ zangs re kun 'dus nyer bzhi yi/ 'khor rnams sna tshogs rol mo bsgyur/ lthags rM sangs rgyas sku gdung gnas/ g.yas bskor g.yon 
11b5(kha): bskor 'dres pa ci/ dper na ce gu bsgrim pa bzhin/ kun s+dzob thams cad g.yon nas te/ don dam shas chi g.yas gnas so// de ltar lha yi dkyil 'khor rnams/ rim par 
11b6(kha): gnas lugs mdor bstan no// mkhas pas yi dbang zhing khams bskyed/ ces gsungs so// kun 'bum go 'byed mngon rtogs rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ dkyil 'khor lha gnas lugs 
12a1(kha): / @/ bstan pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// / de ltar gnas lugs shes byas nas/ dkyil 'khor rgyan gyis brgyan byas nas/ sta gon rim pa gzhung bzhin bya/ dbang dang gdam 
12a2(kha): pa gsal gdab nas/ shes pa goms par bya ba'i phyir/ ting nge 'dzin la gnas pa ni/ rnam pa bzhi ru shes par bya/ dang po rang nyid bsnyen pa'i dus/ bdag s+dzogs kam tshig nad / 
12a3(kha): bgom pa bdag dzogs don du bsgrub pa ni/ dben gnas 'gal rkyen med pa'i sar/ bde bar rang bzhin cha lugs bzhag/ ngag ni dag pa'i sal 'd/ sems bskyed 'gro la pan 
12a4(kha): bya'i phyir/ mngon sangs rgyas pa'i 'dun pa gtang / de nas ma bcos de bzhin nyid/ g.yos kyang tshad med snying rje bskyed/ rgyu yi sa bon rang sems la/ a dkar sal 'd spros pas/ 
12a5(kha): snod ni ren chen g.sung drug dngos/ bcud ni dag pa'i kun 'bum lha/ bsdus pas dus gsum srid gsum gyis/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'i o/ lnga ldan 'od du zhu ba la/ rang

12b1(kha): cang du/ rtsa tlab ye shes zer 'byu'i ste/ nye ma'i dkyil 'khor dmar per 'khyel/ de steng rang sems ngo bo nyid/ 'odi ni cig le gcig tu gsal/ o gyis 'di spros stong gsum 
12b2(kha): sbyangs/ hUM gis sku gsum ye shes bsdus/ de nyid gyur bas kun 'bum sku/ gsal dod mkhyen brtse ldan par bskyed/ de yi thugs kyi dkyil 'khor yang / nyi ma'i da la thig le 
12b3(kha): gsal/ hUM gi mtshan ma sngags kyis bskyor/ gzhan dag lha tshogs gang 'khyud bskyed/ de ltar rang nyid lhar gsal bas/ spyan drang mchod 'brul gnyis med bstam/ rang dbang bya 
12b4(kha): ba'i hUM sgros bshad/ pyi gtsug rtsa ba'i ci bar rgyangs/ kun du bzang pos rgya yi gdab/ oM a dkar sa le 'od/ ngag la snying pos rgya yi gdab/ thugs las ye shes rgya yi gdab//

13a1(kha): hy/ saM/ rang lus yi zhes gnal yas cang / dri med dkyil 'khor lnga ru gyur/ de nas gnas pa'i lha rnams ni/ tcig dbab myur bgyogs ting 'dzin gyis/ dkyil /

13a3(kha): 'khor dbus su dgod par bya'o// o~M a da da ye 'dushA/ bum pa lha yi gzhal yas khang / lha rnams 'di ru 'du ba'i phyir/ gsas mkhar chen po bcu bdun rnams/ ma 'dzil /

13a5(kha): 'khor phyogs bzhir bzhugs su gsol/ ~M ra hUM ba ho shA/ rang 'byung gsal ba'i me long bzniM/ thabs chen 'di dang ldan pa'i phyir/ rig pa'i gnas bzhir byen gyis brlabs/

13b1(kha): 'dul sgo bzhir bzhugs su gsol/ +oM ka ru na khrimshA/ rje rgyal 'tshogs pa'i badan bzhi/ snang sred rlabs kyis gcod pa'i phyir/ rlung lha bzhi ru byin gyis brlabs/ kun /

13b3(kha): sgo bzhir bzhugs su gsol/ o~ he hUM to to ra shA/ dg tags rgyal po 'phan dar bzhaM/ bag chags gtan nas sdug pa'i phyir/ chua lha bni ru byin gyis brlabs/ kun 
13b4(kha): 'dul sgo bzhir bzhugs su gsol/ o~M muru zang na ga daeshA/ bdud las rgyal ba'i rgyal mtshan bzhi/ stobs kyis bdud bzhi 'dul ba'i phyir/ srung gi lha bzhir byin gyis 
13b5(kha): brlabs/ dkyil 'khor sgo bzhir bzhugs su gsol/ oM yaire ma kha bushA/ drang phugs rgyal po mdung shing bni/ thugs rje yo gar med pa'i phyir/ rgyal chen sde bzhir byin 
13b6(kha): gyis brlabs/ dkyil 'khor phyogs bzhir bzhugs su gsol/ o~M ha pe hri sam huns hA/ bder gshegs mchod pa'i yo byad tshogs/ nam mkha'i sprin dpung bzhin du gtib/ 
14a1(kha): / lha rnams thugs dam bskul ba'i phyir/ dkyil 'khor gral la dgod par bya/ oM sal la ha lo sang ngesha/ sems can sbyin pa yas stag tshogs/ sa gzhi'i rtsi 
14a2(kha): bzhin grang mar sungs/ mtha' yas dgos 'dod bskang ba'i phyir/ dkyil 'khor phyi ram spungs par bya/ oM a tha bril du zhi zhes hA/ gnhen rab bla ma 'gro ba'i mgon/ dgongs 
14a3(kha): pa bla na gsal mdzad pa'i/ thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa'i phyir/ chas drug s+dzogs par bzhugs su gsol/ bso ri bu as o~M hU~M pad hAa/ gshen con las mkhan dag 
14a4(kha): pa'i tshogs/ bsam pa 'og nas dag pa yi/ lha dang mi yi brda' sprod phyir/ sum ldan dad pas gnas par bya'o// ~M ha o he o 'dushA/ yin bdag po ma dad pa can/ dge 
14a5(kha): bcu gzung bzhin spyod pa rnams/ dkyil 'khor lha dang mdzal ba'i phyir/ khus kyi bsang nas gnas par bya'o// oM bri ha he hUM ha/ drigs pa'i dbal chas ma bzad pa/

14b1(kha): 'khor dang / rgyan chas dpon gss yin bdag sogs/ ma lus gnas la dgod par bya/ de ni rgyan dgod rim pa'o// 'di gong 'gro ba'i sta gang rnams/ 'di 'og dbang gi skabs nas 
14b2(kha): bton/ zhes gsungs so// kun 'bum rgyud las rgyan dgod bstan pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// de nas ston pas bka' stsal pa/ rang lus rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor du/ mngon

113b3(ca'o): nor med par/ dung thog dkar la bris dag nas/ 'phrul gyi yi ge mkhan znams dang / mtha' yas sems can gang rtsom pa/ bla med go 'phang gdon mi za/ zhes pa'i bslu med g.yung drung gsung //

113b6(ca'o): bdag bcas la/ legs gsol yi rdang phrul tsam gyis/ dge ba'i rsgal pa mnyam 'gyur na/ rnying nas mngon par bstod dang lhan/ gsung gi 'phrin las yel ba yi/ drubs chen dge ba'i rtsa ba /

114a2(ca'o): byang chub nas/ chabs cig mngon sangs rgyas par thog/ lung rtogs bstan pa'i rnying so gang / sring pa'i mthar yang gnas pa dang / res med bstan 'dzin sgkyes bu'i tshogs/ 'gro dan gegs med lhun /

114b4(ca'o): can bd kyi yul du yi go' par khang 'tzugs brkun dang // se gzhi legs bsgrigs byas pa'i 'grems sel yongs khyab byed srel dar zin na'ang / g.yung dung bon gyi ds gzhi'i bsdu bsgrigs byed pa'i ga skabs kyi //
